Chapter One New Boundary

A public carriage came clattering from afar and stopped in front of the gate of a large mansion. The coachman reined in the horse and let down a scantily clad child. Someone opened the fenced gate to welcome him. The child hurriedly asked, "Sir, please tell me, is this Plumfield?"

"Yes, who sent you?"

"Mr. Laurie. I also brought a letter to the lady of the house here."

"Alright; that house, give her the letter; she will take care of you, little shaver."

The man's tone had a pleasant quality. Nat Blake—for that was the child's name—was encouraged by these words and walked along feeling very comfortable. At that time, it was drizzling, sprinkling on the soft grass and budding flowers and trees. Looking from the soft spring rain, Nat saw a large square house in front of him—it had a pleasant and welcoming atmosphere, because it had wide verandas, spacious steps, and many windows, and many lights were shining through the windows. There were obviously no shutters or curtains installed inside, so the joyful light would shine through the windows; before he knocked on the door, he hesitated slightly, seeing countless small shadows dancing on the wall inside, and vaguely hearing the pleasant voices of many teenagers. He thought to himself that such brightness, warmth, and comfort inside the house, a lonely and helpless "little shaver" like him would not be a part of.

Even so, he still thought to himself, "I hope the lady of the house will really take care of me;" so he picked up the big brass knob on the door—in the shape of a laughing old man's head—and knocked lightly.

Then a rosy-cheeked maid opened the door. He silently handed over the letter. She took it, smiling. She seemed used to receiving strange children, because she pointed to a seat in a small room inside the door, nodded to him, and said:

"Sit there and rest on the mat for a while, let me take this to Madam."

While Nat was waiting, he saw many things that were entertaining. He looked around with an excited expression, feeling that the scene was very interesting. At the same time, he secretly rejoiced that he could hide in a corner near the door to observe everything, and he would not be seen by others.

Various Agencies in the City Today Celebrate the Opening of Children's Year: Opening Ceremony Held at the Municipal Government at 9:00 AM; Mayor Wu and Others Inspect Eight Child Care Institutions

National Children's Year is scheduled to open today. Opening ceremonies will be held separately in the central government and various localities. Our city has been prepared by the Children's Year Implementation Committee. The opening ceremony will be held in the auditorium of the Municipal Government at 9:00 AM this morning. There are many programs. The Chinese Children's Culture Association is also scheduled to hold a celebration meeting at the West Shanghai Commune in West Shanghai at 9:00 AM this morning. The details are as follows:

Opening Ceremony to be Held at 9:00 AM

The opening ceremony of Children's Year in our city is scheduled to be held in the auditorium of the Municipal Government at 9:00 AM this morning. The auditorium was decorated yesterday. The presidium of the conference is Mayor Wu and Directors Wu, Pan, Li, and Cai, and one representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters. All participating staff and members of the Implementation Committee must arrive by 8:30 AM and wear Chinese-made clothing to give children a good impression of using Chinese-made goods. The opening ceremony will be completed before 10:30 AM, and Mayor Wu and Director Wu will meet with children's representatives. At the same time, three aircraft will be sent by the Central Aviation School to participate in a flight demonstration.

Transportation Arrangements for Participating Children

In addition to staff, adults are not invited to the opening ceremony. It is estimated that 500 students, 300 orphans, and 200 child laborers will participate, totaling 1,000 people. Thirty people will be divided into a group. Schools, factories, and foster care organizations will send personnel to deliver them to the Municipal Government by car before 8:30 AM. Car fare will be collected from Mr. Guo at the management office of the Preparatory Committee. After the ceremony, the committee will send them back by car.

2,000 Gifts Prepared for Children

In addition to the commemorative badges for the opening of Children's Year presented by Mayor Wu to the participating children today, the committee has collected a total of 2,000 gifts from various manufacturers, all packed in paper bags, one bag per person, and distributed at the opening ceremony, estimated to be more than 1,000 bags. The remaining gifts will be distributed to children in various foster care institutions when the mayor and directors inspect the child care institutions. From 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM in the afternoon, the administrative officials of our city will inspect the child care institutions. The Chinese Children's Culture Association is scheduled to hold a celebration meeting at the West Shanghai Commune on Roberts Road at 9:00 AM this morning, entertaining 700 working and poor children. Kong Xiangxi Addresses the Nation

Kong Xiangxi, Chairman of the China Children's Welfare Association, has specially drafted a book entitled "Respectful Address to the Nation on the Opening Day of Children's Year," which is divided into three paragraphs. The first paragraph describes the history of the establishment of Children's Year: (1) On November 15, 1933, the Children's Welfare Association, based on the suggestion of its Shanghai branch, the Shanghai Children's Welfare Committee, specially requested the National Government to establish a Children's Year system. (2) Starting from March 5, 1935, the 20th meeting of the Executive Yuan of the National Government officially passed the Outline of the National Children's Year Implementation Law jointly drafted by the Minister of Education and the Minister of Interior, deciding that the period from August 1, 1935, to July 31, 1936, would be the implementation period. Thus, the Children's Year system was formally established. The second paragraph discusses the significance of Children's Year: (1) To make everyone have the concept of caring for children and assume the responsibility of caring for children. (2) To make children across the country aware of the importance of their position, strive hard, be self-reliant and unyielding, and be healthy citizens. The third paragraph clarifies the position of the Children's Welfare Association: (1) To lead national children's welfare institutions and organizations to follow the government and promote national children's welfare undertakings. (2) To seek the guidance, criticism, and assistance of the people of the country.

Hubei New Cotton Production Damaged by Floods

Cotton-producing areas in Hubei Province have suffered significant damage due to floods. Recent estimates put production at around 1.8 million dan. Oil Market: White Tung Oil Soars in Hankou, Foreign Firms Sell for 47 Yuan per Dan

The rise and fall of the white tung oil market are entirely tied to the prosperity of exports. This year's foreign trade seems to be more prosperous than in previous years. Therefore, from spring to summer, in the past six months, the price has risen by 14 to 15 yuan per dan. The strength of the rise is unprecedented in the past four or five years. And last week's rise was even more intense. The price of foreign firms in Hankou last week only increased from 39.56 yuan to 40.07 yuan. But since the foreign firms stationed in Hankou started purchasing last week, vying with each other, it was like a scramble, so the price increased every day for a week. It has increased to 47 yuan the day before yesterday. In just one week, it has increased by 6.34 yuan. The strength of the rise has broken the latest record. And all the producing areas have already been almost completely searched by foreign firms. So since the summer, there has been a report of insufficient storage. And recently it is even more so. From the perspective of foreign firms, the demand for goods is still strong, and their efforts to continue are difficult to stop for a while, so the rise in the market cannot be determined. In addition, domestic sales are also starting, and although the number is limited, it does not help its power. It is heard that those who owe money for Zhejiang Tung oil also have to sell for more than 39 yuan per cu, which already shows that things are rare and expensive.

Sugar Market: Chaoqing Sugar Slightly Improves

Yesterday's sugar market, although the tariff was slightly loose, the trend was still tight. The guild's closing price for No. 24 raw granulated white spot was raised by 0.1 yuan to 16.7 yuan, and the price for re-exported goods was 5.1 yuan, but there were no transactions. This factory's cotton white, Zhenyu No. 1 yesterday was 15.8 yuan, and there were transactions. No. 2 was 7 yuan, No. 3 was 5.5 yuan, and No. 4 was 4 yuan. Children's Year and Students' National Goods Year

— Yang An

A large part of the responsibility lies on our little shoulders.

It's exactly: "If you want a prosperous and strong nation, children, mothers must never forget the national goods in their hearts."

Student National Goods Year and University Students

— Ruoyu

The global economic panic of 1928 can be said to have swept across all countries, and it has become more and more intense without any signs of stopping. China, which is backward and has lost all its guarantees, and its industry and commerce, which had only recently begun to develop, have suffered such a blow from this狂潮猛浪. How could they be able to withstand it! Therefore, in recent years, the outflow of large amounts of cash has been like a滔滔不息 river. Watching the snow-white silver in the country dry up day by day, resulting in the decline of industry and commerce and the bankruptcy of rural areas, the entire society has reached a state of universal poverty. People of insight, seeing this dangerous situation, feel that fundamentally promoting national goods is the only way to save the nation and survive. This year is designated as the National Goods Year to take a further step, starting with students, in order to achieve effective results. Because today's Chinese students are generally respected by the people. Although it is no longer as noble as in the old days when "all other professions are inferior, only studying is superior", today's students - especially university students - are still the elite of the country. Their words and actions can still influence the people's eyes and ears, and leading the masses is still a definite fact.

Therefore, during the current Student National Goods Year, how should every student - especially university students - adhere to this purpose and do it practically, as a role model for the people? However, in fact, today's students - especially university students - often cannot achieve this. Usually, in their clothing, food, housing, and transportation, they only see them in Western suits and leather shoes, using foreign goods. They have ended up in the opposite situation. This is truly a painful thing. I say this not without reason, and not to create rumors to sensationalize. Because I recently saw a university professor, and I asked him how the life of today's university students is? He immediately shook his head and said: "It's getting worse and worse. They simply don't want to study more, they just want to get a qualification, find a way out and be done with it. When they first came out of the countryside and entered school, they could still study very hard, and they could still wear old cloth gowns. But after only three months, they all put on Western suits, leather shoes, and filled their hair with Stanco. As for studying, it is becoming increasingly tasteless. Some even spend their days at the ballrooms and pursuing women." After hearing this, I was really a little dazed! At the same time, I thought of this year being the Student National Goods Year, so I unconsciously wrote this passage to reveal it to the people - especially university students. It is best to be able to "correct it if you have it, and strive to do better if you don't." And for the current Chinese situation, we can also carefully reflect on how to use national goods as much as possible in our daily lives and use them as an advocate for the people. Only then will we not fail this Student National Goods Year!

My View on "National Goods Control"

— Xiaobai

The calls for "industrial control" and "economic control" have become increasingly loud recently. Since the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the National Goods League presented a joint petition to the central government last month, requesting the implementation of national goods control, followed by the rubber industry's voluntary request for government control, in the bleak future of national goods, many people have focused on the control of national goods to find a way out. Although, according to general discussion, the benevolent see benevolence, and the wise see wisdom, the praise and criticism of national goods control are still mixed, but everyone undoubtedly attaches importance to the study of implementing national goods control. Therefore, I also dare to express some of my humble opinions here.

At present, most people hold a very skeptical attitude towards whether China should implement national goods control. They believe that our country is a country with backward production, so they are afraid that after the implementation of national goods control, it will affect the free development of the new industry in the bud, and foreign factories in China, due to special relations, will expand instead. This point is indeed worthy of our in-depth study.

However, we must know that the greatest purpose of national goods control is not only to complete the self-sufficiency of national goods in production and consumption, but also to complete the development of foreign trade and oppose the dumping of foreign goods in exchange, and to promote the sharpening of the national goods movement. Therefore, in my opinion, assuming that national goods control can be carried out under the two principles of "planned national goods production" and "self-sufficiency of national goods", it is a very correct direction. Now I will write out my two implementation methods:

1. Active control: For all raw materials and manufactured goods that must be imported from foreigners, we must, under a strict plan, restrict the concentration of the financial resources of the people of the whole country to complete economic self-sufficiency.

2. Passive control: The general new national goods industries that are already growing have suffered greatly in recent years due to excessive free competition. Now we must use the power of the state to implement production control. According to the current state, we must stipulate the production volume and standard prices of each industry and each factory, and limit the disorderly emergence of new factories, so as to adjust and stabilize the foundation of the current national goods industry.

In short, I firmly believe that to implement national goods control, we must pay close attention to the following: First, we must plan and stipulate production so that the production quantity adapts to the consumption quantity and always maintains a balanced state. Second, we must adjust the flow of national goods products and stipulate market prices to achieve the socialization of distribution. Even for competition among the same industry, we must give reasonable control. Third, we must strive to promote the development of foreign markets and at the same time prevent the dumping of foreign goods in China. Foreign factories within the country should also be sanctioned and banned by the government. In this way, I think the current national goods industry shrouded in darkness will have room to rise!

Random Jottings from Yi Lu

— Xu Gan

Before the two words "national goods" were put together to become a noun, I suspected that China didn't produce any goods at all, that it was a completely goods-less country.

That Chinese people have to vigorously promote and urge the use of Chinese goods is truly a rare and comical wonder in the world.

"Promoting national goods" requires designating a "National Goods Year for Women" and a "National Goods Year for Students," making year after year a kind of effective movement; this is also a painstaking method, yet it already causes much astonishment. But if the result of the so-called energetic movement is equivalent to zero, then what else is there to say?

The person selling foreign goods says, "If no one comes to buy, I certainly won't sell them." The person buying foreign goods says, "If no one sells them, I certainly won't buy them." Both are supremely clever answers, but China is ruined by having too many of these clever people.

National goods producers all bitterly resent the national people's ignorance of how to support and cherish them, which prevents national goods manufacturers from competing with foreign merchants. But the general populace resents that national goods manufacturers' products are not as cheap and good as foreign goods, forcing people to purchase foreign goods. Regarding this contradictory situation, I hope both sides can break away from their subjective positions and understand each other.

A fashionable slogan, shouted by those who like to show off for a while, after some time unknowingly turns into stale platitudes. At first, some people might listen to it as a new song, but later, they tire of hearing it, and naturally, those who sing it will also feel less enthusiastic.

Because of the increase in China's trade deficit, money flows out, leading to the daily impoverishment of the national economy and people's livelihoods. But I think there will come a day when impoverishment reaches the point where purchasing power is completely exhausted, and then the trade deficit will definitely decrease, right?

A Visit to the New China Engineering Company

— Huang Jian

Xinzhong is located at Yanjiage, Baoxing Road, Zhabei. Before the January 28th Incident, its capital was 250,000. After the Shanghai Incident, Zhabei was almost destroyed. Fortunately, the factory's employees moved out important machinery beforehand, so although the loss of buildings was still small, the capital for post-war reconstruction was only 150,000, speaking of which, one can't help but feel pained!

Following the factory director Wei Rujun's appointment, I arrived at the factory at eight o'clock the next morning. He personally led the tour, first to the assembly room, which contained more than twenty diesel engines that were either completed, completed but not yet painted, or not yet assembled, with power ranging from ten to seventy-five horsepower. He personally tested a completed unit on the spot, and the results were excellent. When asked about fuel consumption, it was only three pounds per hour, no less than foreign goods. However, because the vibration was very strong, it should only be used in places with solid foundations. It is not suitable for portable water pumps.

Next to the workshop was a water pump testing pool, about two zhang square. At that time, a spiral water pump with a 14-inch diameter was being tested, powered by a 16-horsepower electric motor. It could pump 4,500 gallons of water per hour. It is more cost-effective to use it to pump sewage when the ground difference is not significant. It is especially suitable for inland China to use it with a diesel engine with equivalent horsepower. At that time, a huge stream of water rushed out of the pipe, demonstrating the power of science to mankind.

Arriving at the workshop, drilling machines, planing machines, and washing machines were arranged everywhere. At that time, only three or four people were electric welding cylinders, and one person was repairing the water pump casing on a large planer. The factory cared about the hard work of the workers, so it was a day off as usual. The rest was several engines packed and waiting for shipment, some of which were going to Yunnan.

Turning to the sand casting room, there was one sand casting machine and two iron smelting furnaces. The tools were placed in one place. Like the woodworking room, there was no work due to the holiday, so I did not examine it in detail. I only glanced at it from the window and saw that there were many molds inside, all for sand casting parts.

Further ahead was an open space. Wei Jun said, "We are starting to build an automobile engine research room. After it is completed, we will start work and do our best to contribute to the birth of a national automobile engine." Hearing this, I admired him even more. The factory is making arduous struggles under various difficult conditions, and I sincerely hope that my compatriots will encourage each other so that national goods will not be destroyed by foreign forces!

To the south of the factory is a large material assembly area, prepared for connecting iron bridges and water towers. The Jinhua iron bridge on the Hangjiang Road was built by the factory. Its products are widely sold in Jiangsu, Yunnan, Shaanxi and other places. I hope that its output will increase day by day, so as to celebrate the increasingly bright future of national goods.

Shaoxing Old Wine

— Yi Sun

The large-scale import of foreign wine can't help but remind us of Shaoxing old wine. Now I will write down what I know below:

The reason why Shaoxing wine is mellow can be said to be entirely due to the water. The water used by Shaoxing wineries to brew wine is almost all taken from Jian Lake. This water contains very little salt, phosphoric acid, iron, and other ingredients, and its hardness is only about 2.4, which is very suitable for brewing wine.

The raw materials for brewing wine are glutinous rice, wheat koji, and wine yeast. Glutinous rice is mostly purchased from Wuxi, Danyang and other places. Wine yeast is divided into two types: one is white yeast, which comes from Ningbo; the other is black yeast, which comes from Fuyang. Wheat koji rarely comes from outside the county and is mostly made by local manufacturers.

There are also two methods of brewing wine: one is to spread the rice, and the other is to pour the rice. Because the wine brewed by spreading the rice is more durable, this method is mostly used.

Most wineries are located near Jian Lake, especially concentrated in Ruanshe and Xiguo, with a total of about 1,800. Among them, the most famous are Shen Yonghe, Zhang Dongming, and Wang Youmei. Shen Yonghe invented the use of wine instead of water to brew Shan Niang wine, which tastes quite sweet.

Shaoxing wine sold locally is called Benzhuang; wine sold to other ports is called Luzhuang. Luzhuang wine is mostly transferred to the Pearl River, Yangtze River, and Yellow River basins from Ningbo, Hangzhou, and Shanghai. Some are transported to foreign countries, such as the South Pacific Islands and India, which are also not in the minority.

With a history of two or three thousand years and an annual output of more than 188,000 vats, the scope of Shaoxing wine cannot be considered small; but it can't resist the import of foreign wine. The biggest reason is that the brewers stick to old rules and do not improve. The brewing methods used two thousand years ago are not much different from those currently used. I sincerely hope that the Shaoxing wine industry colleagues will pay attention to this. At the same time, I hope that the government can reduce taxes so that it can compete freely with foreign wine to reverse the outflow of money.

My Opinion on the Handbook for Promoting National Goods

— Zhang Mengzhao

Signature handbooks were popular for a while, leaving a fleeting trace to be cherished for future remembrance!

In ancient times, filial sons cherished utensils left behind by their parents, and today, lovers cherish keeping their loved one's handwriting! Recently, those who socialize have seen the trouble of exchanging business cards and their easy scattering and forgetting! So they compete for signature handbooks, including celebrities, important people, movie queens, and campus beauties! It can be said that "there are golden houses in the book" and "there are beautiful women in the book"!

Unfortunately, exquisite and magnificent handbooks are all imported goods! There are very few handbooks made of national goods. With the wide range of users, the leakage should also be considerable!

I think that the national goods handbook is obviously timely to rise. I hope that paper mills such as Jiangnan and Tianzhang will actively plan. For example, use Jiangnan Lian History with white paper and insert national goods newspapers in the middle so that signatures on the front and back pages will not seep through! The cover is pasted with silk produced by the Maya factory, with various colors, which should be very impressive! Slightly reverse the leakage! Don't do it because of small profits!

The reporter further hopes that celebrities, important people, movie stars, campus beauties, and general social figures, if they encounter non-national goods signature handbooks, should not easily write on them. I sincerely pray with 120,000 points of sincerity!

Shen Bao Special Issue Celebrating the Opening of Children's Year

Opening Speech for Children's Year

— Zhou Shoujuan

Today is the opening day of Children's Year, which is really the most memorable day for children. As the editor of Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly, I have a few sincere words to say to the children.

Children should know that most of those who preside over education and set this Children's Year are middle-aged or elderly people; then why don't they have a middle-aged year or an elderly year, but insist on setting up this Children's Year? Well! This is all because they love you children. Children should also love themselves and cherish their motherland even more.

How to love yourselves? It is to get rid of bad habits and practice a new life; obey your parents' orders at home, and listen to your teachers' instructions at school; work hard at all times to increase your knowledge, cultivate your virtues, and strengthen your physique. Be a well-behaved elementary school student now, and be a great person who benefits the country and the people in the future.

How to love your motherland? It is to recognize the relationship between yourself and the motherland and inspire patriotic thoughts; do not think that you are young and give up the work of saving the country. The first step is to promote national goods to save the country: eat national goods candies and pastries, use national goods stationery and toys, and wear national goods clothes, shoes, and hats. Not only should you use national goods yourself, but you should also persuade others to use national goods. Using one more national good is giving the motherland one more point of vitality. The second step is to pay attention to science to save the country: you must know that the wealth and strength of every country in the world rely on the power of science. A country with backward science will not be able to stand in the world in the future. Therefore, you should put all your energy into science. In elementary school, first lay the foundation of science in arithmetic and natural common sense, and then in middle school and university, you can focus on physics, chemistry, and other subjects, and conduct academic research and practical experiments at any time and place. In the future, inventing new things, opening up new resources, benefiting the people, and strengthening national defense are the best ways to save the country.

Children, today is the first day of Children's Year, so please start doing it step by step from today.

Infant or Old Man?

— Kang Jianzhai Fu

Modern China can be regarded as a decrepit old man, although he is still struggling to rejuvenate. But he is bound by a special environment that does not allow you to open your eyes and speak.

Modern China can also be regarded as a suckling infant, and some ill-intentioned women are vying to be our nannies. They pull on the fat milk on their chests to force you to feed, wanting you to "be like me! be like me!" and not allow you to walk away and learn.

What do we want to do after all?

We are determined not to be decrepit old men waiting for the arrival of death; we are also determined not to always be suckling infants who are manipulated by others. We should of course be lively, strong, free, and independent promising young people.

Lu Fangweng, a patriotic poet of the Southern Song Dynasty, has a poem: "Since ancient times, heroes have had ups and downs, and crises and changes also linger. It is not difficult to resist the poor bandits of Yinping, but to let such a country be given to others?"

Can we give this beautiful country to foreigners?

No! Even if 400 million people die cleanly, we still can't!

Chinese children! Chinese Children's Year!

Don't be a decrepit old man, dying before your eyes;

Don't be a suckling infant, crying and laughing, pitied by others;

Be a lively, strong, free, and independent promising young person!

Good Children in Children's Year

— Yi De

Children! The year starting today is your year, your especially happy year, and your year to enjoy happiness. You see, government offices are open for you, stores are selling at low prices for you, everyone is celebrating for you... the whole society is working hard for you; they are busy for you, and they always say in one sentence that they are all seeking happiness for you.

The so-called good child is not a good child who follows the rules, nor is it a good child who studies hard. You should clearly recognize that our country is a country in urgent national crisis, and the world today is a world where the strong prey on the weak. We should cultivate a unique true spirit to be considered a good child.

How can you be considered a good child? I think first, you must have the spirit of self-improvement. We must go through rational judgment. For what is reasonable, we must sincerely support it. For what is unreasonable, we must stand up to confront it. This precious spirit should be cultivated with care at ordinary times. Second, we must have the spirit of sacrifice: to confront, sacrifice is inevitable; to be afraid of sacrifice is not worthy of confrontation. As long as it is beneficial to the public, we must work hard to do it, sacrificing money, sacrificing happiness, and even sacrificing life, it is not a pity. Otherwise, without the spirit of sacrifice, there will be many considerations when doing things, and with many considerations, the goal of success cannot be achieved. The so-called sacrifice must also have a price. If it is only for personal interests, it is not worth taking at all.

Children! These two spirits are what we lack most, but what we need most urgently. Starting today, please cultivate these two true spirits more, and then be the masters of the country in the future. Today's good children are the good masters of the future.

Children's Year and Modern Parents

— Huang Jiping

The state-designated Children's Year opens today. But we must remember that it is not over with today's celebration, nor does it mean that during this year, people across the country will pay attention to the education of children, and it will be over after this year. It must be known that from now on, after Children's Year, teachers, especially modern parents, must think about the education of children and the happiness of children every year and every moment. In short: (1) Children's daily life, "clothing," "food," "housing," and "transportation," completely rely on the supply of parents, (2) Children's usual cultivation, "wisdom," "virtue," "physical fitness," "group," and "beauty," especially need the guidance of parents: It can be seen that the responsibility of modern parents is really very important, and they simply cannot relax for a moment, and they cannot ignore anything. Thinking back to the past, did ordinary parents ever pay attention to these issues? History tells us that people like Mr. Zhu Baitang, Zeng Wenzheng Gong, Meng Mu, and Yue Mu can be regarded as the most glorious fatherly and motherly teachings: but ordinary people, whether fathers or mothers, only focus on children's "nurturing" - clothing, food, and warmth - and have not studied the "teaching" - the aspects of virtue, wisdom, and physical fitness. Therefore, we reminisce about the past and think that we have not done our best in family education: Thinking about the future, we must never ignore it any longer; parents after Children's Year, in addition to materially supporting children, must add a layer of spiritual guidance, and the latter is much more important than the former.

In our China, whether in cities or villages, families or schools, there are very few rationalized methods and equipment for children's education that can be used as a standard and are worthy of everyone's imitation. Then we can only give others' facts as a reference. In the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, France, Italy, Japan, and Russia, which are known as material civilizations, from the government to the common people, have relatively complete facilities for children's problems in their social organizations. Even the wandering orphans (including lonely, disabled, poor, etc. children) are handled in an orderly manner, unlike the wandering children in our country who live an inhuman life in hell all year round, which is worthy of research. But look at the situation in the UK: "The UK is a kingdom of children" a Japanese educator has already said this. Really, all social life in the UK is centered on children. If you go to a bookstore in London, you can see piles of children's books. Generally, people go to bookstores and always buy a few children's books for their children or buy them as gifts for their friends' children. London citizens are very fond of children and respect children's personality. Even in poor families, there will be a children's room, which is a sacred area, and children become true sovereigns. Of course, that is the kingdom of children, and adults must be very respectful and serious when entering the kingdom. Most families in London have a small garden, and there will be no shortage of children's play equipment. Also, because London is always foggy, which hinders the physical development of children, many people want to move to the suburbs to allow children to get as close as possible to the natural world, which is of course a reflection of the psychology of protecting children. The mothers of British children, for the sake of their children becoming the successors of the British nation, do not hesitate to work hard to train their children in the wind, frost, rain and snow, hoping that they can also raise the banner of the British Empire on the icy island of the North Pole. The British government, society, and families are so attentive to creating well-being for children, which really moves us. In reality, it is not easy to imitate them in our country. But according to my opinion, parents hereafter must not give their children abundant food and clothing and develop their bad habits of pampering themselves; arbitrarily indulging them, gradually leading them into the wrong path of pride, luxury, and licentiousness. They must follow the ancient precepts of "filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame" and make their children work hard in the five aspects of "virtue," "wisdom," "physical fitness," "group," and "beauty," hoping that the future masters will transform the declining China!

Mr. Science Performs Magic Tricks

— He Gongchao

——Burning Characters and Paintings on White Paper——

"Children's Year has opened!" Mr. Science also came to participate in the celebration. Look! He's on stage. He and his assistant are carrying two very large white paper circles onto the stage.

At this time, two chairs were placed in the center of the stage, and they placed these two white paper circles on the backs of the chairs.

"Hello everyone," Mr. Science said after bowing to the audience, "Today is the opening day of Children's Year. I hope that all the children in China, with the help of society and through their own efforts, will create a new child - a new child with a strong body, a scientific mind, and hands that can work. Today, in my magic trick, I will also express a little bit of celebration and encouragement."

After he said that, he called his assistant to take two incense sticks from behind the scenes, lit them with fire, and each held one. Then he continued:

Sure enough, Mr. Science and his assistant lit the top end of the paper with incense, and the paper burned. What was even more surprising was that the fire would move meanderingly on the paper. Before long, a character "Celebrate" appeared, and then a character "Celebrate" appeared. In a short while, the five characters "Celebrate Children's Year" were completely displayed in front of the children.

On another white paper circle, what first appeared seemed to be the top of a person's head. Later, eyebrows appeared, and then eyes, ears, nose, and mouth appeared one after another. It turned out to be a half-length portrait of a smiling child!

The children in the audience watched with interest and applauded continuously.

"Children, do you think this set of magic tricks is interesting? Would you like to try it? It is very suitable to perform this set of magic tricks when schools or families hold celebrations or commemorations. The materials only need three things: (1) a solution of potassium nitrate (available at pharmacies) (it should be a little thicker), (2) thicker white paper, and (3) a fountain pen.

"Once the materials are prepared, use the fountain pen to dip in the solution, write characters or draw pictures on the white paper, and dry it in the shade. The white paper will not show any traces. However, you must make a mark in advance at the starting point to avoid not knowing where to start when performing.

"When performing, use the burning incense to light the paper from the marked place. When you touch a place where the strokes are disconnected, use the incense to light it again. Therefore, the incense should always be held in your hand. - It is best to draw it from beginning to end with one stroke, without any gaps in the middle, so that it can be burned from beginning to end without having to use incense to light it again."

Children's Year and Aviation

— Yunhua

Children's Year! Children's Year! It is our year of happiness, and also our year of hard work! As Ci'er was clapping and singing this song, he suddenly heard a rattling sound in the sky. Looking up, he saw airplanes scattering colorful leaflets celebrating Children's Year. He jumped for joy, his heart filled with indescribable delight. It happened that his teacher, Mr. Li, saw him and called out, "Wang Ci! Why are you so happy?" "Oh, Teacher! I saw the airplanes scattering leaflets to celebrate Children's Year for us children, so I'm especially happy." "That's good. We'll hold an opening ceremony for Children's Year in a little while, and I want you to tell a story about aviation for everyone to hear." Ci'er thought to himself, this is a bit difficult, but how could he disobey the teacher's orders? So he pondered for a long time.

The celebration was very lively, with the principal giving an opening speech, guest speakers, and various performances of songs, dances, music, and sports by students of all grades. Finally, there was a children's speech segment, and Mr. Li introduced Wang Ci to tell a story about aviation. The whole place erupted in applause. Wang Ci walked onto the stage from the crowd, his manner very solemn. He gave a ninety-degree bow and said calmly:

"Principal, teachers, classmates, today is the opening of Children's Year. It may seem irrelevant to speak about aviation instead of children themselves, so please forgive me! Our country's aviation industry is very young and backward. It seems there aren't many stories to tell. I'd like to report on two international aviation news items that perhaps some of you haven't noticed. (1) There is a clever carpenter in France named Mignet who spent many years creating an ingenious airplane. Its structure is simple, and after completion, it was named the "Flying Flea." It is estimated that as many as 10,000 of these can be built in a year, and the French are now widely promoting the functions of the "Flying Flea." (2) Italy and Abyssinia have been preparing for war for a long time, and a bloody battle may be inevitable. Recently, the Italian Air Force has been deployed. Premier Mussolini's sons, aged nineteen and seventeen, have volunteered to join the army and die for their country. The Premier praised them greatly and allowed the two brothers to be the vanguard in the campaign against Abyssinia. Although we do not sympathize with this act of bullying the weak, their youthful ambition and courageous patriotism can serve as a model for us!

Fellow students! In our ranks, I don't believe that there won't be people like the French carpenter and the Italian Premier's sons in the future. If there really aren't, then we are all sinners of the Republic of China!"

Before Wang Ci finished speaking, the applause under the stage was thunderous, and everyone gave him a solemn salute.

Children—this is a lovely, innocent, and hopeful noun full of comfort. It wasn't until the twentieth century that adults realized and changed their previous erroneous concepts of oppressing and despising children to loving and respecting children: knowing that children are important new members of society, not simply miniature adults; and although they cannot directly participate in various social activities now, when their physical and mental development reaches a certain stage, they will also be key players in social activities. This is truly the most fortunate thing in human history.

This is also a bit of what we mean by publishing.

However, the Children's Book Bureau is like a five-year-old child, and its capabilities are still very weak. We hope that educators at home and abroad will provide guidance and support in all our endeavors!

Five Major Problems in Children's Literature

— Pan Gongzhan

—Editing, Selection, Utilization, Guidance, Examination—

Children's literature is the food for children's knowledge. Without food, they will starve! Without suitable food, they will also get sick...

To make children's literature a suitable food for children's knowledge, and one that can be easily digested, we need to solve five problems, namely "the editing and writing of children's literature," "the selection of children's literature," "the utilization of children's literature," "the guidance of children's reading," and "the examination of children's reading."

The editing and writing of children's literature is the most important issue in the study of children's literature. Whether it is the selection of materials, the organization of words, or the composition of the style, everything is sufficient to affect the overall function of the literature. -- How to compile and write literature that is completely suitable for children? This, we should expect from authors and bookstores.

The selection of children's literature arises because the first problem of editing and writing is not fully resolved, and also because in addition to the editing and writing of content, there are various problems such as paper, font, printing, and binding, which may not fully meet our ideals, so when purchasing children's literature, we still need to go through a selection process. -- How to select literature that is completely suitable for children? This, we should expect from schools, families, and bookstores that have the responsibility to publish.

The utilization of children's literature is also an important issue in children's literature. Because children's literature is a kind of tool in education, to make this tool perform its function, there must be a corresponding method of utilization, just like a sharp weapon, in the weapon itself, there is a great function. But to make this weapon show its great function, the first thing is to understand the method of using it, otherwise the weapon itself is simply a dead thing, and it will never exert its great function on its own. -- How to use children's literature? This, we should expect from teachers and parents who have the responsibility to guide children.

The guidance of children's reading is an important issue in increasing the effectiveness of children's reading. The so-called guidance is certainly not teaching word by word, or explaining sentence by sentence, as long as you give detailed instructions on the method of reading, and give a general overview of the content of the literature, so that children will not be at a loss. -- How to give children reasonable guidance? This, we should again expect from responsible teachers and parents.

The examination of children's reading is the final step in diagnosing efficiency. In education, whatever kind of facility is used, what is sought is efficiency: guiding children's reading is a kind of facility in education, and after we implement it, we should of course diagnose it, on the one hand to assess children's reading ability, and on the other hand to measure whether our own guidance methods are appropriate, as a basis for future improvement. -- How to give children a reasonable examination? This, we should again expect from responsible teachers and parents.

In short, to improve children's literature to increase the effectiveness of children's reading, we should work together from all aspects to achieve success.

Speaking of Parent Education from Children's Year

— Liang Shijie

Children are the most lovely and respectable. Their future accomplishments are far greater and more promising than those of any adult. This year, from August 1st to July 31st of next year, is the nationally designated Children's Year. This is what the country means by respecting and hoping for children.

If we respect and hope for children, we must give them a good education. However, a child's lifelong character and temperament are mostly influenced by their parents from a young age. John B. Watson once said: "After observing hundreds of babies, we believe that a person's future model has been formed by the time they are two years old. ... Whether a child will have a noble character in the future? Will they be weak? Will they have many fears? Will they have a violent temper? Will they be emotional or lacking in emotion? ... These questions are already decided in the second year after birth." From this passage, we can know that to respect and hope for children, we should first pay attention to parent education.

The United States is an advanced country, and they spare no effort in promoting parent education. They have: (1) Preparatory parent education -- including "Parent Education" in the curriculum of primary, secondary, universities, and remedial schools, so that unmarried young men and women receive "Parent Education" training: (2) Remedial parent education -- in public and private educational, charitable, religious, academic, and other organizations and institutions throughout the country, organize parent education and child education research associations, or set up parent education training classes, or send people to visit families to investigate the state of child education, or compile and print small booklets on child education to promote it. Looking back at the negligence of "parent education" in China, people can't help but feel dumbfounded. Spencer said: "The survival, death, success, and failure of children all depend on the upbringing of their parents. But the existing education does not mention a word about the parents of children and the methods of child education. Isn't this a strange thing? They completely entrust the fate of children's lives to blind customs and emotional impulses, and then add the opinions of stupid wet nurses or stubborn grandmothers. Isn't this an absurd thing?" These words are aimed at the shortcomings of traditional Chinese family education. May children's welfare organizations and academic groups across the country take advantage of the opportunity of this Children's Year to launch large-scale advocacy and promotion of "parent education"; and hope that parents will study the methods of child rearing!

Timely Children's Science

— Lin Yin

Today is the opening day of Children's Year. Celebrations are being held everywhere, lectures on children's issues are being given everywhere, and children's programs are being broadcast everywhere. Taking advantage of this occasion to study the problem of "sound" in science is definitely not without significance.

Before talking about the principles, we can do a few small experiments to play with. In the experiments, we may understand what sound is. You stand by the edge of a pool or a water tank and use your hand to slap up a few water waves. These water waves will gradually move forward, but when these water waves hit the edge of the tank or the pool, the water waves will immediately return (Figure 1). We can understand that the success of sound is that the air generates waves due to our sound or vibration, just like you use your hand to slap the water. Therefore, the progress of sound is similar to water waves. Therefore, some lecture stages have sounding boards installed above or behind them, which use this effect to make the speaker's sound waves. When the sound waves reach the sounding board, the sound waves will be reflected down and reach the eardrums of the audience, and it will be louder. Some use report microphones to report everything spoken in a large venue (Figure 2). The principle is the same as what I said above. The sound waves hit the edge of the microphone, are reflected down, and mix with the original sound waves, making the sound waves louder and transmitted to the eardrums of the audience.

The situation of sound wave progress has been said above. However, in addition to air, solid things can also transmit sound waves, and they are faster than air. Have you played with a telephone made of matchboxes? (Figure 3) Glue paper to one end of the matchbox, thread a thin wire through it, make two of the same, and you can use them to make a phone call. But you should pay attention, the wire must be pulled tight, otherwise the wire will swing in the air, hindering the progress of the sound waves, and the words will not be heard clearly.

We can also play another experiment. You cover your ears with your hands, teach another person to wrap your head and hands with a hemp rope, and then teach him to hold the two ends of the rope with one hand and pull it tightly, and rub the rope lightly with the fingers of the other hand (Figure 4), then you will hear a very loud sound wave ringing, like thunder. This experiment also proves the example of solid sound transmission.

After a few experiments, we can always understand that sound is a wave formed by air oscillation, its progress is the same as water waves, and solid sound transmission is faster, and when several sound waves combine, it will be louder.

Children's Year Opening Special Issue

Spiritual Construction in Children's Year

— Pan Gongzhan

Today, those who seek the blessings of children are all committed to the construction of material undertakings. In China, where children's undertakings are very weak, this is indeed an effort that we should make. However, the so-called construction of children's undertakings cannot be done by relying on the advocacy of a few people. It must be that the whole country, from top to bottom, has the concept of loving children, and everyone regards loving children as a duty that should be fulfilled, and only through cooperation can we achieve success. Although the children's cause in our country has been advocated for many years, there has been no progress to date, because the people of the country have a weak concept of loving children, fail to regard loving children as a duty to be fulfilled, and fail to fulfill the responsibility of supporting children's undertakings. Therefore, if we want to improve the happiness of children today, in addition to material construction, we should first seek the completion of spiritual construction.

The so-called spiritual construction, in a word, is to promote the concept of loving children among the people of the country. From now on, the government should regard loving children as one of the main governing policies of the country, and regard developing children's undertakings as the top priority of the country. Although the national treasury is empty, special funds should be allocated for loving children. The more difficult the national crisis, the more loving children cannot be abandoned. As for the people, they should know the importance of the status of children and their relationship with the country and the nation, and regard loving children as a natural duty that should be fulfilled by the people. Those with strength should contribute their strength, and those with money should contribute their money. In addition to caring for their own children, they should also care for general children, and "love my young, and extend it to the young of others" should be regarded as a guiding principle. Only then can the meaning of spiritual construction be completed.

After the completion of spiritual construction, the government advocates in the front, and the people support in the back. The construction of material undertakings will be promising. Today is the opening day of the nationally designated Children's Year, and it is the beginning of spiritual construction! I look forward to it!

Thoughts on Children's Year

— Wu Tiecheng

In ancient China, governance and education were combined: nurturing the young and caring for the elderly. This has always been valued. It is true that children have the innate qualities of quick wit and wisdom, pure goodness, and lively nature; their intelligence, virtue, and physical fitness are all above those of adults. If we can teach and nurture them, each in its own way, it will be easy to cultivate them into talents for society and improve the quality of the nation.

In recent times, the trend of political reform in various countries has paid great attention to the protection of people's lives; and children's lives and children's rights are even guaranteed by the constitution. This is evident in the new constitution of Germany after the war. Article 122 of the German Constitution stipulates: "Overwork of children, as well as moral, spiritual, and physical neglect, shall be protected. The Federation, the States, and public organizations shall take the necessary measures for this." Secondly, Articles 119 and 120 also have provisions regarding family hygiene and compulsory education. As for the labor codes of various countries, the protection of children is even more comprehensive, such as working age, working hours, education level, and physical health, all of which are strictly and specially restricted and cared for by law.

Our country's sages did not neglect the issue of children at the beginning. As it is said, "Men have their duties, women have their homes, the strong are employed, the young are nurtured, and the widowed, orphaned, lonely, disabled, and sick are all cared for," and "Men have their duties, women have their homes, the strong are employed, and love my young, and extend it to the young of others." Their spirit of caring for and paying attention to children can be imagined. It is a pity that in recent times, education has been neglected, and not only the state and society have neglected children; even parents and elders do not know their responsibility for education and upbringing. They live together all day long, and their words do not touch on righteousness: their behavior is dissolute, and their minds and bodies deteriorate day by day. Children are the future spirit of the nation and the cornerstone of the country. If this continues without attention, the harm it will cause to the nation and the country is unimaginable.

Now, on the opening day of the National Children's Year, I would like to briefly express my feelings during my spare time. I deeply hope that those who are engaged in the children's movement today will pay close attention to and study children's psychology, children's education, children's thoughts, children's habits, children's morality, children's bodies, children's lives, children's hygiene, and children's welfare, so that countless lively, pure, and intelligent children will not be corrupted by bad environments, but will be cultivated into talents for the country and society. Then their contribution to the future of our nation will be immeasurable!

Notice to All Children in the City

— Shanghai Children's Year Implementation Committee

Adorable children of the whole city!

Today is the opening day of the National Children's Year. Our committee, bearing the responsibility of implementing the Children's Year in this city, naturally wants to take this opportunity to say a few words to all the children in the city.

Our China has designated April 4th as Children's Day, and from today until July of next year, it is also designated as Children's Year. The central government advocates from above, and various provinces and cities promote from below. Such emphasis on children is such a memorable thing. Especially on this opening day of Children's Year, which is the beginning of the implementation of the year's work, everyone should celebrate the arrival of children's welfare with joy and excitement.

Moreover, the Children's Year was initiated by the China Child Welfare Association in this city, and the implementation measures for the Children's Year were also drafted by the Children's Welfare Committee in this city? It can be seen that this city has a special significance for the Children's Year.

"Children are the foundation of the nation, the inheritors of society, and the pillars of the country." Everyone knows these words, and everyone can say them. Children's position in the nation, their position in society, and their position in the country are of great importance. At the same time, the children's future responsibility to the nation, their responsibility to society, and their responsibility to the country are equally important!

We believe that children in cities, because of the easy access to educational opportunities, the influence of material civilization, and the great power of environmental change, their inherent knowledge is often superior to that of ordinary rural children in the inland. Shanghai is the area where culture of our country converges, and it is one of the six major commercial ports in the world. The total population of the city reaches 3,533,597 (according to the statistics of the Municipal Public Security Bureau in June of this year). Furthermore, considering the number of school-age children in the city (special zone to be investigated), which reaches 110,675 (according to the survey conducted by the Municipal Education Bureau in the 22nd year of the Republic of China), it is estimated that the total number of children in the city is probably no less than 800,000, a number that exceeds any other city in the country. In this vast society that contains so many children, we hope that all the children in Shanghai will work hard to make progress and become the leaders of children in all provinces and cities across the country in the future!

Children: are not the private property of the family; they are a part of the society, the nation, and the country. The children of today are the part of the society, nation, and country that will bear responsibility in the future. Therefore, how much attention should families and society pay to the protection and education of children, so that they can take on the responsibility of inheriting the past and opening up the future.

We, the members of this committee, are not talented, but since we bear the responsibility of implementing the Children's Year, we have to do our best diligently. We have drafted an implementation plan, the main points of which are: (1) urging society to pay attention to children's issues; (2) promoting children's welfare undertakings; (3) improving children's education; (4) striving for the relief of abandoned children, illegitimate children, and children with disabilities. At the same time, promoting the general awareness of children about their own position and understanding the difficulties of our country's future. However, this significant responsibility cannot be undertaken by a few people, so we have to hope that all citizens will work together to help achieve this great mission.

Declaration of the China Child Welfare Association

Today is the official opening day of Children's Year. On the national level, under the leadership of Chairman Lin, there are enthusiastic and grand celebrations in various places. On the Shanghai level, under the leadership of Mayor Wu, the city has excellent and magnificent performances. Adults are certainly watching children, expressing sincere care, and all the children are celebrating their second birthday with joy. This is truly a unique phenomenon since the establishment of the Republic of China, a moment worthy of special mention in Chinese history. Recalling that on March 7th of the 20th year of the Republic of China, our association requested the establishment of a Children's Day system, and on November 15th of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, we requested the establishment of a Children's Year system. Under the circumstances of frequent incidents and numerous urgent matters, the two requests made by our association were adopted and promulgated by the government. This is truly something that fills our country with gratitude and excitement. Under the leadership and promotion of the wise government, coupled with the efforts and struggles of the people of the whole country, we believe that the happiness of Chinese children is boundless, and the development of the Chinese nation is even more boundless. The current depressed situation certainly makes our hearts ache; but when we see the emerging generation about to rise up, following our bloodstained footsteps to march towards the battle line for the survival of the nation, we cannot help but feel infinite comfort and infinite hope. How strictly communist-led Russia is training their Young Pioneers, how seriously fascist-led Italy is training their Boy Scout groups, how diligently the National Socialist Party-led Germany is training their youth groups, and how hard other countries such as England, America, France, and Japan are working to educate their children. We advocate that the motherland led by the Kuomintang should also use the same strictness, seriousness, diligence, and effort to train and educate our children. This is the great way to save the country, and it is also the basic work of cultivating great citizens. We believe that our compatriots across the country will agree with this. The government's outline of the National Children's Year implementation measures, which should be carried out during Children's Year, already contains very detailed instructions. Our association should follow the people of the country and hope to promote its thorough realization. The opening day of Children's Year is the day when children's welfare undertakings begin; but children's welfare undertakings are endless and will never end with the expiration of Children's Year. Therefore, we believe that the entire nation should bear the responsibility for children's welfare undertakings forever. The "education" and "nurturing" of children should be the full responsibility of the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior. As for how to contact and coordinate with children's welfare organizations, academic research institutions, medical and health institutions, and people who sympathize with children's welfare undertakings across the country, following the government to work hard to complete the construction of children's welfare, this responsibility seems to be our association's inescapable duty. In today's transitional era, our association is aware of the great responsibility it bears and will certainly strive forward diligently; but because the responsibility is heavy and the road is long, and the task is difficult, we hope that the people of the country will provide the most severe supervision, the most candid instructions, and the most effective assistance at any time!

Slogans for Children's Year

(1) General Slogans (Ten items)

Children's Year is the beginning of the children's century. Children's Year is the initial foundation for the revitalization of the nation. Children's happiness originates in Children's Year. Children are the buds of human civilization. Children are the new seedlings of national life. Children are the little masters of the Republic of China. Children are the little angels of the family. New children create a new China. Love the country, starting with loving children. Respect the personality and human rights of children.

(2) Slogans on Protecting Children and Relieving Poor Children (Ten items)

Fully protect child labor. Thoroughly improve the apprenticeship system. Absolutely prohibit keeping maids. Eradicate the demons who abuse children. Strictly arrest the bandits who abduct and sell children. Relieve the vast majority of abandoned children and orphans. Do not allow a single homeless child in the country. Equal treatment for boys and girls. Arrest infanticide criminals. Arrest the Jianghu thugs who injure and disable children to make them perform and sell their skills.

(3) Slogans on Children's Welfare Organizations

Modernize infant asylums. Improve poor children's homes... Widely establish public nurseries. Widely establish work-study groups to accommodate homeless children. Open theaters and cinemas for children. Widely establish children's libraries. Widely establish children's playgrounds. Universally organize permanent children's welfare associations.
